function medic_heal(first_speaker, second_speaker)
  db.actor.health = 1
  db.actor.power = 1
  db.actor.radiation = -1         
  first_speaker:heal_wounds(1.0)
end

function fix_flags()
    local sobj = alife():object("esc_wolf")
    if sobj then
                local pk = get_netpk( sobj, 1 )
                ASSERT( ( pk and pk:isOk() ), "can't read netpacket of %s", sobj:name() )
                local data = pk:get()
                    data.visual_name = "actors\\neytral\\stalker_neytral_rukzak_3" --–≤–∏–∑—É–∞–ª
                pk:set( data )
    end
end

function start_set_bandit (trader, actor)
dialogs.relocate_item_section(trader, "wpn_pm", "in")
dialogs.relocate_item_section(trader, "bandit_master_outfit", "in")
dialogs.relocate_item_section(trader, "device_pda_bandit", "in")
dialogs.relocate_item_section(trader, "wpn_bm16", "in")
dialogs.relocate_item_section(trader, "ammo_12x70_buck", "in")
end
